false\n    68→\t}\n    69→\tif err != nil {\n    70→\t\tv.errors = append(v.errors, err)\n    71→\t}\n    72→\treturn true\n    73→}\n    74→\n    75→func (r *RBACAuthorizer) Authorize(ctx 99→\t\t\t\tb.WriteString(requestAttributes.GetSubresource())\n   100→\t\t\t}\n   101→\t\t\tb.WriteString(`\"`)\n   102→\t\t\tif len(requestAttributes.GetName()) > 0 {\n   103→\t\t\t\tb.WriteString(` spans multiple critical components across the plugin and pkg directories:\\n\\n## RBAC Authorizer (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go)\\nThe `RBACAuthorizer` struct implements the core authorization logic through its `Authorize` method. This method receives authorization requests and evaluates them against RBAC policies. The authorizer delegates rule resolution to a `RequestToRuleMapper` interface, which is implemented by `DefaultRuleResolver`.\\n\\n## Subject Access Evaluator (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go)\\nThe `SubjectAccessEvaluator` is a component that evaluates which subjects (users, groups, service accounts) are allowed to perform specific actions. It implements the `SubjectLocator` interface and provides the `AllowedSubjects` method to determine which subjects can perform an action based on role bindings and the rules they reference.\\n\\n## Default Rule Resolver (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go)\\nThe `DefaultRuleResolver` is the core component that resolves PolicyRules for users. It implements the `AuthorizationRuleResolver` interface with three key methods:\\n- `RulesFor`: Returns all rules applicable to a user in a namespace\\n- `VisitRulesFor`: Iterates through rules with a visitor pattern, supporting early short-circuiting\\n- `GetRoleReferenceRules`: Resolves role references from RoleBindings and ClusterRoleBindings to their actual PolicyRules\\n\\nThe resolver accumulates rules from both cluster-wide ClusterRoleBindings and namespace-scoped RoleBindings, gathering all applicable roles and their contained rules.\\n\\n## SubjectAccessReview REST Handlers\\nThree REST handlers expose the authorization system to API clients:\\n- `pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go`: Cluster-scoped handler for evaluating arbitrary subjects\\n- `pkg/registry/authorization/localsubjectaccessreview/rest.go`: Namespace-scoped handler for evaluating subjects within a namespace\\n- `pkg/registry/authorization/selfsubjectaccessreview/rest.go`: Handler for users to check their own permissions\\n\\nAll handlers instantiate a `REST` struct that uses the `Authorize` method to evaluate the request and return a `SubjectAccessReviewStatus` with allowed/denied decision and reason.\\n\\n## Bootstrap RBAC Policies\\nThree files define bootstrap RBAC policies loaded at cluster startup:\\n- `plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/policy.go`: Base bootstrap policy definitions\\n- `plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/controller_policy.go`: Policies for system controllers (node, kubelet, kube-proxy, etc.)\\n- `plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/namespace_policy.go`: Default namespace-scoped roles (edit, view, admin)\\n\\nThese are loaded through `pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go` via the `PostStartHook` mechanism to establish default roles and bindings.\\n\\n## Escalation Prevention\\nThe escalation prevention system uses multiple layers:\\n\\n1. **Escalation Checks** (pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go):\\n   - `EscalationAllowed`: Checks if user is in system:masters group (superuser)\\n   - `RoleEscalationAuthorized`: Verifies explicit authorization to escalate roles\\n   - `BindingAuthorized`: Verifies user can bind a specific role reference\\n\\n2. **Policy-Based Storage** with escalation validation:\\n   - `pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go`: Prevents users from creating/updating Roles with permissions they don't have\\n   - `pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go`: Prevents privilege escalation through RoleBindings\\n   - `pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go`: Prevents privilege escalation through ClusterRoles, including aggregation rules\\n   - `pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go`: Prevents privilege escalation through ClusterRoleBindings\\n\\n3. **Escalation Validation Functions**:\\n   - `ConfirmNoEscalation` (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go): Validates that rules don't grant permissions beyond what the user already has\\n   - `ConfirmNoEscalationInternal` (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/internal_version_adapter.go): Converts internal rbac types to v1 before validation\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\nAdditional files provide supporting functionality:\\n- `pkg/registry/rbac/validation/policy_compact.go`: Compacts rules for efficient comparison\\n- `pkg/registry/rbac/helpers.go`: Utility function `IsOnlyMutatingGCFields` to detect garbage collection mutations\\n- `pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go`: Main REST storage provider that coordinates policy-based storage for all RBAC resources\\n\\n## Authorization Flow\\nThe complete authorization chain: RBACAuthorizer.Authorize → VisitRulesFor → DefaultRuleResolver.VisitRulesFor → GetRoleReferenceRules (to get rules from Role/ClusterRole) → RuleAllows (to match request against rules). During create/update operations, policy-based storage wrappers intercept to validate escalation rules using ConfirmNoEscalation to ensure users cannot grant themselves elevated permissions.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1505,"cache_read_input_tokens":62626,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1505},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"294766b6-3910-48c1-a7cc-4aec3142ae18","uuid":"8495babb-da3c-472a-8160-efbc54de9797"}
